INNER JOIN `cycle` AS `c0` ON `c`.`cycle_id` = `c0`.`id`

    WHEN `s0`.`start` > @__now_1 THEN 1
    WHEN `s0`.`start` < @__now_1 THEN -1

    WHEN `s0`.`end` = @__now_1 THEN 0
    WHEN `s0`.`end` > @__now_1 THEN 1
